_citizens for legitimate government httpwwwlegitgovorgdc_madam_update_260907html 1 of 3 522008 803 am subpoenas served on abcs brian rossnew york posts cindy adams by dc madam by lori price wwwlegitgovorg 26 sep 2007 breaking clg exclusive citizens for legitimate government clg has learned that socalled dc madam deborah jeane palfrey has issued subpoenas for the depositions of i troy burrus the irs case agent on palfreys case for friday september 28th in washington dc and ii brian ross of abc news ii cindy adams of the new york post and iv bill bastone of the smoking gun for friday october 5th in new york city jeane palfrey told lori price the civil process is far more liberal one for defendant than its criminal counterpart perfect example is mr sibleys reference in his email blast this afternoon whereby witnesses can be deposed before trial in civil action but not in criminal concern this is simply fantastic since the first involves merely moneyproperty whereas the second involves an individuals actual liberty had judge kessler conducted the civil phase of my overall case appropriately and i daresay legally last fall the civil case never would have been stayed mr sibley acting as my civil lawyer then would have been given the opportunity to uncover the muck in my case in the more open civil arena and subsequently i never would have been indicted criminally had i been given my rightful due process here this ordeal would not have lived much past the new year regarding judge kesslers seeming disregard for my welfare i frankly have answer for why she has behaved the way she has from the onset of my case last year my best and only guess is an overt disdain she that has for mr sibley currently we are attempting to recuse judge kessler for her unprecedented attempt to bar mr sibley from acting as my criminal attorney the past few weeks judge kessler has stepped so far over the line in this particular instance as to allow the government to weigh in on why mr sibley should not represent mr sibley in his research cannot find single case where the judge in casecitizens for legitimate government httpwwwlegitgovorgdc_madam_update_260907html 2 of 3 522008 803 am has not permitted defendant to have counsel of hisher choice because of the courts personal wishes from montgomery blair sibley jeane palfreys attorney along with the criminal case against jeane palfrey the government has also filed civil forfeiture action seeking to take all her assets curiously in the criminal action in which palfrey could go to jail she is not allowed to gather information before trial by examinations of witnesses under oath however in the civil forfeiture action such discovery before trial is allowed go figure judge kessler stopped the civil forfeiture action last march for six months to prevent palfrey from getting information to help her defense in the civil and criminal cases that stay order expired last week and i promptly issued subpoenas for the depositions of i troy burrus the irs case agent on palfreys case for friday september 28th in washington dc and ii brian ross of abc news ii cindy adams of the new york post and iv bill bastone of the smokinguncom for friday october 5th in new york city those subpoenas were served yesterday on the witnesses i expect both the government and the subpoenaed witnesses to aggressively fight palfreys attempt to get the basic information regarding why this matter was commenced by the government and how the government has acted since the seizing of all palfreys assets one year ago heaven forbid the truth comes out 26 sep 2007 email this page to friend the url for this page httpwwwlegitgovorgdc_madam_update_260907html previous dc madam news and updates dc madam defense likely to disclose evidence identities deemed classified by lori price 01 sep 2007 citizens for legitimate government has learned that deborah jeane palfrey the dc madam has filed with the court pro motion for pretrial conference to consider matters relating to classified information under the classified information procedures act this filing alerts the government that palfreys defense will likely involve the disclosure of evidence and identities presently deemed classified by the us government dc madam phone records by lori price 09 jul 2007 citizens for legitimate government
